 ) madhya pradesh kii ichhaavar vidhansabha seat sihor jile main aati he
 Ichhawar is located at a distance of 57 km from the capital Bhopal
 yah sitbijepika garh he, haalanki 2013 ke chunaav main use haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa tha
 One more thing about Ichawar is special
 kaha jaataa he ki jo mukhyamantri ichhaavar kaa daura karata he usko kursi ganvaani padati he
 And history also tells something similar
 is baat kaa andaja aap isse laga saktaa hai ki khud siem shivaraj singh bataur siem rahete iske ilaake main nahin aae hai
 Let me tell you that many Chief Ministers have tried to break the myth of Ichawar, but all the Chief Ministers who stepped here had to lose their chair
 2003 main tatkaaleen mukhyamantri digvijay singh ne bhi is myth ko todane ke liye 15 november, 2003 ko yojit sahakaari sammelan main shaamil hone ichhaavar pahunche the
 After this, the Congress had to face a crushing defeat in the elections held in Madhya Pradesh
 ichhaavar ke myth ko todane kii koshish mukhyamantri dow
 Kailash Nath Katju also did
 katju 12 janvari 1962 ko vidhansabha chunaav ke ek kaarykram main bhaag lene ichhaavar aae the or iske baad 11 march 1962 ko hue vidhansabha chunaavon main congress haar gai or dow
 Kailash Nath Katju had to be defeated by his power
 vahiin 1 march 1967 ko dwarka prasad mishra bhi ichhaavar aae the or 7 march 1967 ko hue nae mantrimandal ke gathan se upje asantosh ke chalate mishra ko mukhyamantri pad se istipha dena padaa
 2013 and 2008 election results In the 2013 elections, Shailendra Ramesh Chandra Patel of Congress defeated bjp's Karan Singh Kanhaiyalal by just 744 votes
 2008 ke chunaav main bijepi ke karan singh verma ne congress ke dow
 Balveer Tomar was defeated by over 18 thousand votes
 is chunaav main karan singh tomars ko 50129 vot mili the to vahiin dow
 Balveer Tomar received 31977 votes
 2013 main kya the rajya ke chunavi nattijeymadhya pradesh main kul 231 vidhansabha siten hai
 Elections are held on 230 seats while one member is nominated
 2013 ke chunaav main bijepi ko 165, congress ko 58, basapa ko 4 or anya ko teen siten mili thim

 You enjoyed plenty of free videos on youtube but, now get ready to pay
 darasal, lakhon videos or karodon yugers vaali ye website jald hi aapse paisa vasuulana shuru kar degi
 This website is completely free since its launch
 isamen videos dekhne ke liye koi charge nahin lagata he or yahi isaki lokapriyata kaa sabase bada kaaran bhi he
 Currently youtube does not take any money from those who upload videos and watch them
 yani ki isamen koi bhi video aplod kar saktaa he or use dekh bhi saktaa he
